# List Agents

**URL:** https://docs.ultravox.ai/api-reference/agents/agents-list

## Description
Returns details for all agents

## Endpoint
```
GET /api/agent
```

## Request/Response Examples

data-component-part="field-meta"><div class="flex items-center px-2 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-gray-100/50 dark:bg-white/5 text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-200 font-medium break-all" overflow-wrap-anywhere [&amp;_*]:overflow-wrap-anywhere"><p class="whitespace-pre-line">The minimum amount of time the agent will wait to respond after the user seems to be done
speaking. Increasing this value will make the agent less eager to respond, which may increase
perceived response latency but will also make the agent less likely to jump in before the user
is really done speaking.</p>
<p class="whitespace-pre-line">Built-in VAD currently operates on 32ms frames, so only multiples of 32ms are meaningful.
(Anything from 1ms to 31ms will produce the same result.)</p>
<p class="whitespace-pre-line">Defaults to &quot;0.384s&quot; (384ms) as a starting point, but there&#x27;s nothing special about this value
aside from it corresponding to 12 VAD frames.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="primitive-param-field border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-b last:border-b-0"><div class="py-6"><div class="flex font-mono text-sm group/param-head param-head break-all relative" id="response-results-items-call-template-vad-settings-minimum-turn-duration"><div class="flex-1 flex flex-col overflow-wrap-anywhere [&amp;_*]:overflow-wrap-anywhere"><p class="whitespace-pre-line">The minimum duration of user speech required to be considered a user turn.
Increasing this value will cause the agent to ignore short user audio. This may be useful in
particularly noisy environments, but it comes at the cost of possibly ignoring very short
user responses such as &quot;yes&quot; or &quot;no&quot;.</p>

built-in noise cancellation).</p></div></div></div></div><div class="primitive-param-field border-gray-100 dark:border-gray-800 border-b last:border-b-0"><div class="py-6"><div class="flex font-mono for built-in tools (though it&#x27;s possible for third-party tools that wrap a

[&amp;_div]:inline [&amp;_div]:mr-2 [&amp;_div]:leading-5" data-component-part="field-meta"><div class="flex items-center px-2 py-0.5 rounded-md bg-gray-100/50 dark:bg-white/5 text-gray-600 whitespace-normal prose prose-sm prose-gray dark:prose-invert overflow-wrap-anywhere [&amp;_*]:overflow-wrap-anywhere"><p class="whitespace-pre-line">JSON schema for the variables used in string templates. If unset, a default schema will
be created from the variables used in the string templates.
Call creation requests must provide context adhering to this schema.
The follow fields are treated as templates:</p>
<ul class="list-inside list-disc whitespace-normal" data-streamdown="unordered-list">
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">system_prompt</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">language_hint</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">time_exceeded_message</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">inactivity_messages.message</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">selected_tools.description</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">selected_tools.static_parameters.value</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">selected_tools.http.auth_headers.value</li>
<li class="py-1 [&amp;&gt;p]:inline" data-streamdown="list-item">selected_tools.http.auth_query_params.value
If multiple stages are defined for the call, each must define its own context schema (or use the generated one).</li>
</ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></details></div></div></div></div></div></div></details></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="primitive-param-field border-gray-100
